Param/Value/E0A70EE9=<s val="ModCenterSize24Bold"><c val="00FF00">Hunter</c></s><n/><n/><s val="ModCenterSize16Bold">This is both a guide on How to Play, and How to Use Hunter. Hunter can be one of Zealots most powerful allies if used correctly. <n/><n/><c val="00FF00">Search for bases:</c> Hunter should always be on the prowl for more targets for Zealot, if you find one don't try to Feed for your own income unless you know where at least 5 bases are, Probes are ALWAYS moving around, keep looking.<n/><n/><c val="00FF00">Check Golds:</c> don't let Zealot waste his time checking Gold Bases, Hunter is the most beneficial role to check Golds, if a Probe is there it becomes easy feed for Zealot, but in most cases you will get a bit of Minerals and hurt Probe economy by destroying Miners<n/><n/><c val="00FF00">Give Zealot Resources:</c> after you buy 200 Mineral boots, give Zealot all your resources until end game, he needs them more than you.<n/><n/><c val="00FF00">Give Hunter Resources:</c> late game Hunters can double, triple, or more Zealot income, don't let them go to waste, Zealot giving your Hunter even just 2-4 Gas can change a game massively in your favor.</s>
